END AS pinlei,CASE WHEN a.item_number != '' THEN e.title WHEN a.specification_id != '' THEN e.title ELSE '未匹配' END AS guige,a.product_name AS aproduct_name,CASE WHEN a.item_number != '' THEN a.item_number ELSE '无款号' END AS item_number,a.xiangqian AS axiangqian,b.quantity as kucun,b.jinzhong AS bjinzhong,a.single AS asingle,a.weight AS aweight,CASE WHEN b.kufang = '0' THEN '总库' ELSE g.title END AS bkufang,CAST(ROUND( h.cost_price, 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 10, 2 )) AS ecost_price,CAST(ROUND( h.sales_price, 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 10, 2 )) AS esales_price,CAST(ROUND( h.basic_cost* a.jin_zhong, 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 10, 2 )) AS echengben,CAST(ROUND( h.company_surcharge, 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 10, 2 )) AS echengbenfj,CAST(ROUND( h.premium_cost * a.jin_zhong, 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 10, 2 )) AS ecankao,CAST(ROUND( h.sales_cost* a.jin_zhong, 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 10, 2 )) AS exiaoshou,CAST(ROUND( h.sales_surcharge, 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 10, 2 )) AS esales_surcharge,i.shitou as shitou,i.stnum as shishu,i.shitou1 as fushitou,i.shnum1 as fushishu,a.state as astate,a.remarks AS aremarks FROM xipunum_erp_shop_kucun AS b  INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_shop AS a ON a.poduct_code =b.poduct_code  LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_ksiamges AS c ON c.kuanhao = a.item_number LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_category AS d ON d.id = c.category_id LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_specs AS e ON e.id = a.specification_id LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_category AS f ON f.id = e.category_id  LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_type AS g ON g.id = b.kufang AND b.kufang != '0' INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_store AS h ON h.poduct_code = a.poduct_code LEFT JOIN 执行SQL语句 (全_MySQL读取, 到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (相加 (“SELECT tol.chukudanhao AS tol_chukudanhao,tol.chukutime AS tol_chukutime,tol.kufang AS tol_kufang,CAST(ROUND(sum(tol.shuliang), 2) AS DECIMAL (20, 2)) AS tol_shuliang,CAST(ROUND(sum(tol.jinzhong), 3) AS DECIMAL (20, 3)) AS tol_jinzhong,CAST(ROUND(tol.hsjinzhong, 3) AS DECIMAL (20, 3)) AS tol_hsjinzhong,CAST(ROUND(sum(tol.yingshou), 2) AS DECIMAL (20, 2)) AS tol_yingshou,CAST(ROUND(tol.hsjine, 2) AS DECIMAL (20, 2)) AS tol_hsjine,CAST(ROUND( tol.youhui, 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS tol_youhui,CAST(ROUND(tol.shishou, 2) AS DECIMAL (20, 2)) AS tol_ssjine,CAST(ROUND(sum(tol.chengben), 2) AS DECIMAL (20, 2)) AS tol_chengben,CAST(ROUND(sum(tol.xsgongfei), 2) AS DECIMAL (20, 2)) AS tol_xsgongfei,CAST(ROUND(sum(tol.xsfujia), 2) AS DECIMAL (20, 2)) AS tol_xsfujia,CAST(ROUND(tol.shuie, 2) AS DECIMAL (20, 2)) AS tol_shuie,CAST(ROUND(tol.kegongfei, 2) AS DECIMAL (20, 2)) AS tol_kegongfei,tol.pling AS tol_pling,tol.yewu AS tol_yewu,tol.daogou AS tol_daogou,CONCAT(tol.fcjuser, '(', tol.mingcheng, ')') AS caozuo,tol.ddid AS tol_ddid,tol.zhuangtai AS tol_zhuangtai,tol.kmemberid AS tol_kmemberid,tol.kname AS tol_kname,tol.jieshao as jieshao FROM (SELECT i.settlement_number AS chukudanhao,i.creationtime AS chukutime,CASE WHEN a.kufang = '0' THEN '总库' ELSE h.title END AS kufang,a.quantity AS shuliang,a.net_weight AS jinzhong,COALESCE(l.jin_zhong, 0) AS hsjinzhong,a.settlement AS yingshou,COALESCE ( l.retreat_amount, 0 ) AS hsjine,CASE WHEN a.sales_return = 1 THEN -i.youhui ELSE i.youhui END AS youhui,i.settlement as shishou,CASE WHEN a.sales_return = 0 THEN CASE WHEN a.quantity != 0 THEN e.cost_price * a.quantity ELSE e.cost_price END WHEN a.sales_return = 1 THEN CASE WHEN a.quantity = 0 THEN - e.cost_price ELSE - e.cost_price * a.quantity END ELSE 0 END AS chengben,CASE WHEN a.quantity < 0 THEN - a.sales_cost*a.net_weight ELSE a.sales_cost*a.net_weight END AS xsgongfei,a.sales_surcharge AS xsfujia,i.taxamount AS shuie,a.sales_cost AS kegongfei,i.pling AS pling,i.salesman AS yewu,n.name AS daogou,m.NAME AS mingcheng,i.cjuser AS fcjuser,i.id AS ddid,i.state AS zhuangtai,k.memberid as kmemberid,k.name as kname,o.name as jieshao FROM xipunum_erp_outbound AS a INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_shop AS b ON b.poduct_code = a.poduct_code LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_category AS c ON c.id = b.category_id LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_specs AS d ON d.id = b.specification_id INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_store AS e ON e.poduct_code = b.poduct_code LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_type AS h ON h.id = a.kufang INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_outbound_order AS i ON i.id = a.order_id LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_member AS k ON k.customer_code = i.customer_code LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_retreat_order AS l ON l.retrea_umber = i.retrea_umber INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_user AS m ON m.USER = i.cjuser INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_user AS n ON n.USER =a.shopping_guide LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_member AS o ON o.memberid =i.shopping_guide WHERE (i.settlement_number LIKE '%”, 查找信息文本内容, “%' or k.memberid LIKE '%”, 查找信息文本内容, “%' or k.name LIKE '%”, 查找信息文本内容, “%' or k.tel LIKE '%”, 查找信息文本内容, “%') ”, 查找信息库房名称, 查找销售检索, “ AND i.creationtime >= '”, 查找信息开始日期, “' AND i.creationtime < '”, 查找信息结束日期, “' ORDER BY i.creationtime DESC ) AS tol GROUP BY  tol.ddid ORDER BY tol.chukutime asc”)), #编码_GBK, #编码_UTF_8, )))

执行SQL语句 (全_MySQL读取, 到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (相加 (“SELECT a.memberid as amemberid,a.customer_code AS acustomer_code,a.NAME AS aname,a.tel AS atel,ROUND(IFNULL(c.cun_number, 0) - IFNULL(c.qian_number, 0), 3) AS jieyuliao,ROUND(IFNULL(d.cun_number, 0) - IFNULL(d.qian_number, 0), 2) AS jieyuyuan,a.shengri AS ashengri,a.dizhi AS adizhi,a.cjuser AS acjuser,a.creationtime AS acreationtime,b.NAME AS bname,COALESCE(e.cq_min_creationtime, a.creationtime) as zxtime  FROM xipunum_erp_member AS a INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_user AS b ON b.USER = a.cjuser LEFT JOIN ( SELECT  customer_code, SUM(CASE WHEN cunqu = '存' AND type = '料' THEN number ELSE 0 END) AS cun_number, SUM(CASE WHEN cunqu = '欠' AND type = '料' THEN number ELSE 0 END) AS qian_number FROM xipunum_erp_member_cq  WHERE kufang in (”, 全局_店铺权限操作, “) AND type = '料' GROUP BY customer_code ) AS c ON c.customer_code = a.customer_code LEFT JOIN ( SELECT  customer_code, SUM(CASE WHEN cunqu = '存' AND type = '元' THEN number ELSE 0 END) AS cun_number, SUM(CASE WHEN cunqu = '欠' AND type = '元' THEN number ELSE 0 END) AS qian_number FROM xipunum_erp_member_cq  WHERE kufang in (”, 全局_店铺权限操作, “) AND type = '元' GROUP BY customer_code ) AS d ON d.customer_code = a.customer_code LEFT JOIN (SELECT customer_code,max(creationtime) AS cq_min_creationtime FROM xipunum_erp_member_cq WHERE kufang IN (”, 全局_店铺权限操作, “) AND type IN ('料', '元') GROUP BY customer_code) AS e ON e.customer_code = a.customer_code WHERE a.customer_code IN ( SELECT DISTINCT customer_code FROM (SELECT customer_code FROM xipunum_erp_outbound_order WHERE cjuser IN ”, 全局_全局查看, “ UNION SELECT customer_code FROM xipunum_erp_retreat_order WHERE cjuser IN ”, 全局_全局查看, “ UNION SELECT customer_code FROM xipunum_erp_presale_order WHERE cjuser IN ”, 全局_全局查看, “ UNION SELECT customer_code FROM xipunum_erp_member WHERE cjuser IN ”, 全局_全局查看, “ ) AS combined WHERE customer_code != '' AND customer_code IS NOT NULL ) AND (a.customer_code LIKE '%”, 查找信息文本内容, “%' OR a.NAME LIKE '%”, 查找信息文本内容, “%' OR a.tel LIKE '%”, 查找信息文本内容, “%' OR a.dizhi LIKE '%”, 查找信息文本内容, “%') ORDER BY a.customer_code asc”)), #编码_GBK, #编码_UTF_8, )))

    集_数据报表.获取明细网格 ().获取数据集 ().获取字段集合 ().获取项目 (到变体型_文本型 (“商品款号”)).置字符值 (到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (订单详情款号), #编码_UTF_8, #编码_GBK, )))
    集_数据报表.获取明细网格 ().获取数据集 ().获取字段集合 ().获取项目 (到变体型_文本型 (“品类”)).置字符值 (到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (订单详情品类), #编码_UTF_8, #编码_GBK, )))
    .如果 (不等于 (订单详情圈口, “”))
        集_数据报表.获取明细网格 ().获取数据集 ().获取字段集合 ().获取项目 (到变体型_文本型 (“规格”)).置字符值 (到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (相加 (订单详情规格, “ ”, 订单详情圈口, “#”)), #编码_UTF_8, #编码_GBK, )))
    .否则
        集_数据报表.获取明细网格 ().获取数据集 ().获取字段集合 ().获取项目 (到变体型_文本型 (“规格”)).置字符值 (到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (订单详情规格), #编码_UTF_8, #编码_GBK, )))
    .如果结束

.子程序 _临时销售_获取数据, , ,

.局部变量 查询列表计次, 整数型, , , 
.局部变量 查询列表临时单号, 文本型, , ,

.局部变量 查询列表销售数量, 文本型, , ,

赋值 (查找信息文本内容, 窗口_主窗口.局部_查询内容)
赋值 (查找信息库房名称, 窗口_主窗口.局部_库房名称)
.如果 (不等于 (窗口_主窗口.局部_库房名称, “”))
    赋值 (查找信息库房名称, 相加 (“ and a.kufang ='”, 窗口_主窗口.局部_库房名称, “'”))
.否则
    赋值 (查找信息库房名称, 相加 (“ and a.kufang in (”, 全局_店铺权限操作, “)”))
.如果结束
执行SQL语句 (全_MySQL读取, 到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (相加 (“SELECT a.number AS anumber,b.title AS kufang,CAST(ROUND( sum( a.quantity ), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS aquantity,CAST(ROUND( sum( a.net_weight ), 3 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 3 )) AS anet_weight,CAST(ROUND( sum( a.xiao_amount ), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS axiao_amount,CAST(ROUND( sum( CASE WHEN a.quantity != 0 THEN c.cost_price * a.quantity ELSE a.net_weight/d.jin_zhong*c.cost_price END ), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS chengben,CAST(ROUND( sum( a.net_weight*a.sales_cost ), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS xsgongfei,CAST(ROUND( sum( a.sales_surcharge ), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS xsfujia,CONCAT( a.cjuser, '(', e.name, ')' ) AS chuangjian FROM erp_outbound AS a INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_type AS b ON b.id = a.kufang INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_store AS c ON c.poduct_code = a.poduct_code  INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_shop AS d ON d.poduct_code = a.poduct_code INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_user AS e ON e.USER = a.cjuser WHERE a.number LIKE '%”, 查找信息文本内容, “%'”, 查找信息库房名称, “ GROUP BY a.number ORDER BY a.number ASC;”)), #编码_GBK, #编码_UTF_8, )))
